</td></tr>

</td></tr>
<tr><td valign='top' style='width:473.4pt;padding-left:5.4pt;padding-right:5.4pt'><p style='font:10pt Times New Roman;margin:0;color:#000000'>On April&#160;27, 2021, the Board declared a dividend on the Company&#8217;s outstanding common stock; outstanding 6.125% Perpetual Preferred Stock, Series&#160;C Depositary Shares; outstanding 5.375% Preferred Stock, Series D Depositary Shares; outstanding 5.875% Preferred Stock, Series E Depositary Shares; and outstanding 6.125% Series F Depositary Shares.</p>
<p style='font:10pt Times New Roman;margin:0;color:#000000'>&#160;</p>
<p style='font:10pt Times New Roman;margin:0;color:#000000'>In addition, on April 27, 2021, the Board called for redemption on June 15, 2021 (the &#8220;Redemption Date&#8221;) of all of its outstanding depositary shares representing a 1/40th interest in a share of the Company&#8217;s 6.125% Perpetual Preferred Stock, Series C (the &#8220;Series C Depositary Shares&#8221;). &#160;There are currently 2,600,000 Series C Depositary Shares outstanding. The Series C Depositary Shares will be redeemed at a redemption price of $25 per Series C Depositary Share, plus an amount equal to any declared and unpaid dividends to the Redemption Date.</p>
<p style='font:10pt Times New Roman;margin:0;color:#000000'>&#160;</p>
<p style='font:10pt Times New Roman;margin:0'>The press release issued by the Company on April 27, 2021 relating to the foregoing information is attached hereto &#160;as Exhibit 99.1 and is incorporated herein by reference.</p>

</TD><TD valign=top style=width:342pt;padding-left:5.4pt;padding-right:5.4pt><P style='font:24pt Arial;margin:0'><B>NEWS RELEASE</B></P>
<P style='font:12pt Arial;margin:0'>&nbsp;</P>

<P align=center style='font:10pt Arial;margin:0;text-indent:-9pt;margin-left:-4.5pt'>&nbsp;</P>
<P style='font:10pt Arial;margin:0'><KBD style='position:absolute;text-align:right;font:10pt Times New Roman;width:481.5pt;border-bottom:1px solid #000000'></KBD>&nbsp;</P>
<P style='font:10pt Arial;margin:0'>&nbsp;</P>
<P align=center style='font:16pt Arial;margin:0;text-indent:-9pt;margin-left:-4.5pt'><B>Associated Announces Annual Meeting Results, Dividends, and Redemption of Depositary Shares Representing Interests in 6.125% Perpetual Preferred Stock, Series C</B></P>
<P align=center style='font:16pt Arial;margin:0'>&nbsp;</P>
<P style='font:10pt Arial;margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-left:-13.5pt;margin-right:-8.1pt'><B>GREEN BAY, Wis. </B>&#8211;&#8211; April 27, 2021 &#8211;&#8211; Associated Banc-Corp (NYSE:ASB) (&#8220;Associated&#8221;) today announced the results of the actions taken at its 2021 Annual Meeting of Shareholders.</P>
<P style='font:10pt Arial;margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-left:-13.5pt;margin-right:-8.1pt'>The following directors were re-elected:</P>
<P style='font:10pt Arial;margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-right:-8.1pt'><KBD style='position:absolute;font:10pt Arial;margin-left:0pt'>&#45;</KBD><KBD style=margin-left:36pt></KBD>John (Jay) B. Williams, chairman, Associated Banc-Corp, and chairman, Church Mutual Insurance
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Company&nbsp;</P>
<P style='font:10pt Arial;margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-right:-8.1pt'><KBD style='position:absolute;font:10pt Arial;margin-left:0pt'>&#45;</KBD><KBD style=margin-left:36pt></KBD>Philip B. Flynn, president and chief executive officer, Associated Banc-Corp&nbsp;</P>
<P style='font:10pt Arial;margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-right:-8.1pt'><KBD style='position:absolute;font:10pt Arial;margin-left:0pt'>&#45;</KBD><KBD style=margin-left:36pt></KBD>John F. Bergstrom, chairman and chief executive officer, Bergstrom Corp.&nbsp;</P>
<P style='font:10pt Arial;margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-right:-8.1pt'><KBD style='position:absolute;font:10pt Arial;margin-left:0pt'>&#45;</KBD><KBD style=margin-left:36pt></KBD>R. Jay Gerken, director of 19 mutual funds associated with Sanford C. Bernstein Fund, Inc.&nbsp;</P>
<P style='font:10pt Arial;margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-right:-8.1pt'><KBD style='position:absolute;font:10pt Arial;margin-left:0pt'>&#45;</KBD><KBD style=margin-left:36pt></KBD>Judith P. Greffin, former chief investment officer, Allstate Corporation&nbsp;</P>
<P style='font:10pt Arial;margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:6pt;margin-right:-7.9pt'><KBD style='position:absolute;font:10pt Arial;margin-left:0pt'>&#45;</KBD><KBD style=margin-left:36pt></KBD>Michael J. Haddad, chair of the board of directors, Schreiber Foods, Inc.&nbsp;</P>
<P style='font:10pt Arial;margin:0;margin-right:-8.1pt'><KBD style='position:absolute;font:10pt Arial;margin-left:0pt'>&#45;</KBD><KBD style=margin-left:36pt></KBD>Robert A. Jeffe, senior operating partner, BlackWatch&nbsp;</P>
<P style='font:10pt Arial;margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-right:-8.1pt'><KBD style='position:absolute;font:10pt Arial;margin-left:0pt'>&#45;</KBD><KBD style=margin-left:36pt></KBD>Eileen A. Kamerick, adjunct professor of law and consultant&nbsp;</P>
<P style='font:10pt Arial;margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-right:-8.1pt'><KBD style='position:absolute;font:10pt Arial;margin-left:0pt'>&#45;</KBD><KBD style=margin-left:36pt></KBD>Gale E. Klappa, executive chairman, WEC Energy Group&nbsp;</P>
<P style='font:10pt Arial;margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-right:-8.1pt'><KBD style='position:absolute;font:10pt Arial;margin-left:0pt'>&#45;</KBD><KBD style=margin-left:36pt></KBD>Cory L. Nettles, founder and managing director, Generation Growth Capital, Inc.&nbsp;</P>
<P style='font:10pt Arial;margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-right:-8.1pt'><KBD style='position:absolute;font:10pt Arial;margin-left:0pt'>&#45;</KBD><KBD style=margin-left:36pt></KBD>Karen T. van Lith, CEO of APEL Worldwide, LLC&nbsp;</P>
<P style='font:10pt Arial;margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-left:-13.5pt;margin-right:-8.1pt'>Shareholders also (1) gave advisory approval to named executive officer compensation, and (2) ratified the selection of KPMG LLP as Associated&#8217;s independent accounting firm for 2021.</P>
<P style='font:10pt Arial;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-left:-13.7pt'><B>Dividends</B></P>
<P style='font:10pt Arial;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-left:-13.7pt'>The Associated Board of Directors declared a regular quarterly cash dividend of $0.18 per common share, payable on June&#160;15, 2021, to shareholders of record at the close of business on June 1, 2021. </P>
<HR style='border:0;height:0;width:0;margin:14pt 0 0 0'><HR style='page-break-after:always;border:0;height:3pt;background-color:#909090;margin:8pt 0'><P style=line-height:0;margin:0></P>
<HR style='border:0;height:0;width:0;margin:14pt 0 0 0'><P style='font:10pt Arial;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-left:-13.7pt'>The Board of Directors also declared a regular quarterly cash dividend of $0.3828125 per depositary share on Associated Banc-Corp&#8217;s 6.125% Series C Perpetual Preferred Stock, payable on June 15, 2021 to shareholders of record at the close of business on June 1, 2021.</P>
<P style='font:10pt Arial;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-left:-13.7pt'>The Board of Directors also declared a regular quarterly cash dividend of $0.3359375 per depositary share on Associated&#8217;s 5.375% Series D Perpetual Preferred Stock, payable on June 15, 2021 to shareholders of record at the close of business on June 1, 2021.</P>
<P style='font:10pt Arial;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-left:-13.7pt'>The Board of Directors also declared a regular quarterly cash dividend of $0.3671875 per depositary share on Associated&#8217;s 5.875% Series E Perpetual Preferred Stock, payable on June 15, 2021 to shareholders of record at the close of business on June 1, 2021.</P>
<P style='font:10pt Arial;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-left:-13.7pt'>The Board of Directors also declared a regular quarterly cash dividend of $0.3515625 per depositary share on Associated&#8217;s 5.625% Series F Perpetual Preferred Stock, payable on June 15, 2021 to shareholders of record at the close of business on June 1, 2021.</P>
<P style='font:10pt Arial;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:6pt;margin-left:-13.7pt'><B>6.125% Perpetual Preferred Stock, Series C Redemption</B></P>
<P style='font:10pt Arial;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:6pt;margin-left:-13.7pt'>In addition, the Board called for redemption on June 15, 2021 (the &#8220;Redemption Date&#8221;) of all of its outstanding depositary shares (NYSE: ASB PR C) representing a 1/40th interest in a share of Associated&#8217;s 6.125% Perpetual Preferred Stock, Series C (the &#8220;Depositary Shares&#8221;). &nbsp;As of today, there are 2,600,000 Depositary Shares outstanding. The Depositary Shares will be redeemed at a redemption price of $25 per Depositary Share, plus an amount equal to any declared and unpaid dividends to the Redemption Date. </P>
<P style='font:10pt Arial;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:6pt;margin-left:-14.4pt;margin-right:-7.9pt;background-color:#FFFFFF'>A notice of redemption and related materials will be transmitted to holders of record of the Depositary Shares on April 27, 2021. The Depositary Shares are held through The Depository Trust Company (&#8220;DTC&#8221;) and will be redeemed in accordance with the procedures of DTC. &nbsp;Payment to DTC will be made by Equiniti Trust Company, in accordance with the Deposit Agreement among Associated, Wells Fargo Bank, N.A. (now known as Equiniti Trust Company) and the Holders from Time to Time of the Depositary Receipts Described Therein, dated as of June 8, 2015. &nbsp;<A name=_Hlk68951205 />Questions related to the notice of redemption and related materials should be directed to Equiniti Trust Company,<B> </B>as Associated&#8217;s redemption agent (the &#8220;Redemption Agent&#8221;), at 1-800-468-9716. The Redemption Agent&#8217;s address is Equiniti Trust Company, Attn: Corporate Actions Department, 1110 Centre Pointe Curve Suite 101, Mendota Heights, MN 55120.</P>
<HR style='border:0;height:0;width:0;margin:14pt 0 0 0'><HR style='page-break-after:always;border:0;height:3pt;background-color:#909090;margin:8pt 0'><P style=line-height:0;margin:0></P>
<HR style='border:0;height:0;width:0;margin:14pt 0 0 0'><P style='font:10pt Arial;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:6pt;margin-left:-14.4pt;margin-right:-7.9pt;background-color:#FFFFFF'><B>ABOUT ASSOCIATED BANC-CORP</B></P>
<P style='font:10pt Arial;margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-left:-13.7pt;margin-right:-7.9pt'>Associated Banc-Corp (NYSE: ASB) has total assets of $35 billion and is one of the top 50, publicly traded, U.S. bank holding companies.&#160;Headquartered in Green Bay, Wisconsin, Associated is a leading Midwest banking franchise, offering a full range of financial products and services from more than 220 banking locations serving more than 120 communities throughout Wisconsin, Illinois and Minnesota, and commercial financial services in Indiana, Michigan, Missouri, Ohio and Texas. Associated Bank, N.A. is an Equal Housing Lender, Equal Opportunity Lender and Member FDIC. More information about Associated Banc-Corp is available at <FONT style='color:#0000FF;border-bottom:1px solid #0000FF'>www.associatedbank.com</FONT>. </P>
<P align=center style='font:10pt Arial;margin:0;margin-left:-14.4pt;margin-right:-7.9pt;background-color:#FFFFFF'>&nbsp;</P>
<P style='font:10pt Arial;margin:0'>&nbsp;</P>

var Show={};Show.LastAR=null,Show.showAR=function(a,r,w){if(Show.LastAR)Show.hideAR();var e=a;while(e&&e.nodeName!='TABLE')e=e.nextSibling;if(!e||e.nodeName!='TABLE'){var ref=((window)?w.document:document).getElementById(r);if(ref){e=ref.cloneNode(!0);
e.removeAttribute('id');a.parentNode.appendChild(e)}}
if(e)e.style.display='block';Show.LastAR=e};Show.hideAR=function(){Show.LastAR.style.display='none'};Show.toggleNext=function(a){var e=a;while(e.nodeName!='DIV')e=e.nextSibling;if(!e.style){}else if(!e.style.display){}else{var d,p_;if(e.style.display=='none'){d='block';p='-'}else{d='none';p='+'}
e.style.display=d;if(a.textContent){a.textContent=p+a.textContent.substring(1)}else{a.innerText=p+a.innerText.substring(1)}}}
